	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: action.php');
	writefile_7();
	if (!is_file('action.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): action.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('action.php') != '2b9e2847592ea422fc7575f4b92dafc087d2a499') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): action.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('action.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of action.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('action.php') !== '2b9e2847592ea422fc7575f4b92dafc087d2a499') {
		if (@sha1_file('action.php') !== 'a08601f8f9e64c53bfbc60ed2f440d508150515c') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: action.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('action.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('action.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('action.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_7();
		if (@sha1_file('action.php') !== '2b9e2847592ea422fc7575f4b92dafc087d2a499') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): action.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('setup/sql/struct.sql')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/sql/struct.sql');
	writefile_17();
	if (!is_file('setup/sql/struct.sql')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/sql/struct.sql');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/sql/struct.sql') != 'f9ddb729f250dfaf9b47cd8cba270612ba6272b4') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/struct.sql');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/sql/struct.sql', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/sql/struct.sql');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/struct.sql') !== 'f9ddb729f250dfaf9b47cd8cba270612ba6272b4') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/struct.sql') !== '193bf33c6cf3a7314e532f89cf5da1157d0538b5') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/sql/struct.sql');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/sql/struct.sql');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/sql/struct.sql')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/sql/struct.sql', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_17();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/struct.sql') !== 'f9ddb729f250dfaf9b47cd8cba270612ba6272b4') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/struct.sql');
		}
	}
}

			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/sql/wellknown_ids.sql');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/sql/wellknown_ids.sql');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/sql/wellknown_ids.sql')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/sql/wellknown_ids.sql', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_18();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_ids.sql') !== '51df9ff02dc2217a6d523c261b5044182bb34b3b') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/wellknown_ids.sql');
		}
	}
}

} else {
	if (@sha1_file('whois/webwhois.php') !== '51f7a4945e1668f22bf7b74ffe99e869731d2b15') {
		if (@sha1_file('whois/webwhois.php') !== '52299d5daa7fb961a86bcba6894be2ae0163027a') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: whois/webwhois.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('whois/webwhois.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('whois/webwhois.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('whois/webwhois.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_19();
		if (@sha1_file('whois/webwhois.php') !== '51f7a4945e1668f22bf7b74ffe99e869731d2b15') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): whois/webwhois.php');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('oidplus_version.txt', "Revision 13\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 13') err('Could not write to oidplus_version.txt!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3

@unlink(__FILE__);
if (is_file(__FILE__)) warn('Could not delete '.basename(__FILE__).'! Please delete it manually');
